  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_46677070-8ab6-48f9-a752-ab0759885a7d'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();

The thing with the thieving and use of powers gives it away. As does the mention<a href="#" rel="nofollow noopener">…more</a>
    *******SPOILERS AHEAD*******<br />-<br />-<br />-<br />-<br />-<br />-<br />-<br />-<br />-<br />-<br />-<br />-<br />-<br />-<br />-<br />-<br />It was definitely Magpie. The thing with the thieving and use of powers gives it away. As does the mention of the bullet that Nova grabbed from her by accident. My jaw about hit the floor once I figured out that she was actually Evie. I'm seriously hoping there is a sequel series in the works!!! There doesn't seem to me to be a whole lot of point to the epilogue as it was written if there isn't. Stirring interest and the desire to know more instead of neatly wrapping everything up seems cruel to me.<a href="#" rel="nofollow noopener">(less)</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer13464913289797143683"><blockquote>
  <b>What if the lines weren’t so clearly drawn? What if she wasn’t either a hero or a villain? What if she was both?<br/></b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>Wow, so I finally got my hands on this book!<br/><br/>I’m leaving up all of my theories up at the bottom of my review because that’s what 99% of the comments on this review are in reference to. It feels weird to delete them now even though I’ve read the book because then everyone’s comments on here won’t make sense. So while they are left up, that doesn’t mean that any of my theories were ri</span>
  <span id="freeText13464913289797143683" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>What if the lines weren’t so clearly drawn? What if she wasn’t either a hero or a villain? What if she was both?<br></b>
</blockquote><br><br>Wow, so I finally got my hands on this book!<br><br>I’m leaving up all of my theories up at the bottom of my review because that’s what 99% of the comments on this review are in reference to. It feels weird to delete them now even though I’ve read the book because then everyone’s comments on here won’t make sense. So while they are left up, that doesn’t mean that any of my theories were right or wrong. Don’t read into them still being here!<br><br><b>All that being said, here’s my actual review:</b><br><br>I really enjoyed this book. RENEGADES is one of my favorite YA series. It’s all about good versus evil. About forming your own opinions and not just believing everything your parents and the government tells you. It has some romance and some found family. <b>It’s sweet and wholesome and violent and morally grey. </b>It’s great!<br><br>The beginning of the book is action packed, but the middle was reallllly slow. Slower than any part of the previous books. But the last third of the novel is so fast paced it makes up for the slow middle third!<br><br>I feel so bad because Nova is constantly being manipulated by everyone around her. <b>I just want to teleport myself into this world and give her a hug (and hope that she doesn’t stab me in response). </b><br><br>This was a great ending to the series. <b>I loved how it addressed everything from abuse of power to prison reform to worker’s rights to challenging leaders to recognizing that your parents’ views aren’t always right. </b>I do wish a few plot points were wrapped up better at the very end, but overall it was a great end to the trilogy! I love how the ending sets up the potential for a spin-off series. <br><br>Side note: The artist who drew this specified on their post not to repost their work anywhere so I’m just giving the link instead of adding the image but this (and the rest of their Nova/Adrian artwork) is what I picture Nova and Adrian to actually look like (not the official artwork which makes them all look 30): <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://itme-z.tumblr.com/post/171515540741/i-just-had-to-draw-one-of-my-favorite-scenes-from">https://itme-z.tumblr.com/post/171515...</a>.<br><br><b>Content Warnings and Trigger Warnings:</b> mentions of child sexual assault by family friend, violence, blood, gore,torture, death, grief, <br><br>————————————————————<br><br><b>[everything below this is has nothing to do with my actual review. it is just a bunch of theories for what i thought might happen in SUPERNOVA. i am not going to say which, if any, of these theories were correct. this portion is left up since this is what most of the comments on the review are referring to. feel free to skip it.]</b><br><br>————————————————————<br><br><b>February 07, 2019</b><br>WE HAVE A TITLE!!!!!!!! <br><br>SUPERNOVA <br><i>and</i> our MC is named <i>NOVA</i> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462882835ra/19055505.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="A GIF from the Disney Pixar movie The Incredibles which says Coincidence? I think not!" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>November 08, 2018:</b><br><br><b>Okay, brace yourself for THEORIES. (This contains spoilers for the first two books)</b><br><br>If we don't fucking get the big reveal with Captain Chromium and Dread Warden and Adrian and Nova and in one place I WILL FUCKING RIOT. I craveeee that drama. Like *surprise* your son's first girlfriend kind of tried to kill you.<br><br>I can't wait for Nova to be all "Well it's because you didn't save my family" and them to be all "well, <i>actually</i> it was your uncle's fault" and Nova to be all "no! you're lying!!" and Adrian be all "no, they are telling the truth" and then Nova go all psycho-killer on Ace. <br><br>Also, can't wait for Danna to lead her swarm of butterflies back to Nova's house and everyone be all confused and a huge fight occur and Nova gets caught.<br><br>And Adrian will have to go all Sentinel and his dads will find out. <br><br>I can't wait for Nova to realize the helmet was meant for her the whole time. Also what's up with the bracelet trying to connect to it?!? What's the meaning of the star Adrian kind of made her that got attached to her bracelet? Magpie said it's super valuable. Is it....dare I say....love? (ha! so cheesy) <br><br>Can't wait for Max to wake up and be like "that Nightmare chick lowkey saved my life....also have you notice how her perfume smells like Nova's?"<br><br>If I don't learn who killed Adrian's mom or Phobia's backstory I will declare this whole series a waste of my time.<br><br>Theories I had after the first book THAT WERE NEVER ADDRESSED:<br>-Either Phobia and Ace totally dated or Phobia is Adrian's bio-dad. (It would explain the note and why his mom could never reveal his true dad). OR BOTH.<br>-Max stole Adrian's mom's power, that's how she died. Hugh and Simon found out about Max that way when she fell to her death. It's why they were so adamant about taking them in.<br>-Also I picture Max as someone who drains a battery not steals a power. Because of the whole Ace ending thing. Where Max could drain a person of their power (keeping it if he doesn't use it daily) and the prodigy has to recharge and still has their power.<br>-Ace hired a hitman because Nova's parents were working with the Renegades. Ace blamed it on a rival gang. The whole "loyalty" and "the Renegades will come" and "they must be stopped" speeches her parents gave makes me think they were totally helping the Rengades. Also her dad hid her power from Ace because he knew Ace would want her for the cause.<br>~OR~<br>-Ace didn't hire the hitman. The hitman was actually a Renegade sent to hurt Ace via his fam. Either way, their deaths seem shadier than the Roaches killing them...</span>

<div id="review_3036011036" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3036011036" />
    <a title="jessica" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10171516-jessica"><img alt="jessica" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1509983330p2/10171516.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3036011036?book_show_action=true">Nov 06, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="jessica" class="user" itemprop="url" name="jessica" href="/user/show/10171516-jessica">jessica</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3036011036" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2573552189585310232">this is definitely the best book in this series. i am not a fan of superhero stories, so i have no idea how i have made it to the end of this trilogy, but i am so happy this ends the way it does. <br/><br/>the significant difference between this last installment and its predecessors is the character development. in the first two books, everything is black/white, good/evil, hero/villain, friend/foe, etc. but this book finally gives the characters some wiggle room to venture into that grey area in between. </span>
  <span id="freeText2573552189585310232" style="display:none">this is definitely the best book in this series. i am not a fan of superhero stories, so i have no idea how i have made it to the end of this trilogy, but i am so happy this ends the way it does. <br /><br />the significant difference between this last installment and its predecessors is the character development. in the first two books, everything is black/white, good/evil, hero/villain, friend/foe, etc. but this book finally gives the characters some wiggle room to venture into that grey area in between. it allows for human complexity that isnt quite present in the first two books, and i think that this new characterisation is a great asset to how this story is resolved. <br /><br />i will admit the action scenes still feel a little cheesy to me - literally all that is missing is a POW or BAM in little balloon bubbles down the margins - but the nonstop pacing makes this go by very quickly. the story hits the ground running on the first page and doesnt stop until the end of epilogue.<br /><br />i think many fans of this series will be beyond satisfied with this conclusion. i know i am!<br /><br /><b>↠ <i>3.5 stars</i></b></span>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

<span id="freeTextContainer11744826834902008459"><b>First of all, I called it. I figured it out and you can bet I'm smug about it.</b><br/><br/>Second of all, this book is totally going to have another sequel right? Like, there is no other way but for it to have a sequel? A spinoff maybe? A six-book series? Will it ever end? Will the battle between good and evil ever be won by either side? Idk. But you can bet I'm down to find out!<br/><br/>In this "final" installment all the build-up finally has it's payoff and all the epicness that had been hinted at before is finally</span>
  <span id="freeText11744826834902008459" style="display:none"><b>First of all, I called it. I figured it out and you can bet I'm smug about it.</b><br /><br />Second of all, this book is totally going to have another sequel right? Like, there is no other way but for it to have a sequel? A spinoff maybe? A six-book series? Will it ever end? Will the battle between good and evil ever be won by either side? Idk. But you can bet I'm down to find out!<br /><br />In this "final" installment all the build-up finally has it's payoff and all the epicness that had been hinted at before is finally showed. We finally see Ace Anarchy be the badass he was always mentioned to be. We see the full extent of Captain Chromiums powers and of each of the character's abilities.  And of course, we see the epic final showdown that is the battle for Galton!<br /><br /><b>Also, we see the relationships that are at the base of this story. Adrian's relationship with his adoptive fathers and brother is absolutely everything. And Nova's complex relationship with her uncle and the remaining Anarchists was so wonderful and twisted and I loved every second of it.</b><br /><br />This review is all over the place and its because my emotions are everywhere and I have forgotten how to use words. Bear with me.<br /><br />This book was good y'all. I have to admit, book one felt long-winded and like nothing more than an overdrawn out introduction to the world and characters. Book two was fairly entertaining. This book though? This is where it's at. It was 550 pages long and I was hooked through every single one of them!<br /><br /><b>Overall, this was such a satisfying conclusion. And such a great and subtle beginning to the new age of hero!</b><br /><br />Follow Me Here Too:<b> <a href="http://www.thebookcovergirls.wordpress.com" rel="nofollow noopener">My Blog</a> || <a href="https://twitter.com/covergirlreads" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> || <a href="https://www.bloglovin.com/blogs/book-cover-girl-19339391" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Bloglovin'</a> || <a href="https://www.instagram.com/thebookcovergirls//" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> || <a href="https://thebookcovergirls.tumblr.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Tumblr</a> || <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/thebookcovergirls/" rel="nofollow noopener">Pinterest</a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="11744826834902008459" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audiobook 9781250232199" href="/book/show/49000738-supernova">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16254355-matthew?shelf=gr_awards_2019">gr_awards_2019</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2712774603" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12200837287435855548">Supernova is a decent ending to the newest series from Marissa Meyer. I enjoyed the journey with all the characters and her interesting spin on the super hero genre.<br/><br/>I did not enjoy it quite as much as The Lunar Chronicles, but I would not take that to heart to much. It was a very tough task to follow up after that series and I think she did just about as good as she possibly could. I am sure that fans of that series will also find a lot to like here.<br/><br/>If you have not tried Marissa Meyer before but</span>
  <span id="freeText12200837287435855548" style="display:none">Supernova is a decent ending to the newest series from Marissa Meyer. I enjoyed the journey with all the characters and her interesting spin on the super hero genre.<br><br>I did not enjoy it quite as much as The Lunar Chronicles, but I would not take that to heart to much. It was a very tough task to follow up after that series and I think she did just about as good as she possibly could. I am sure that fans of that series will also find a lot to like here.<br><br>If you have not tried Marissa Meyer before but you like any combination of the following, I am pretty sure you should go ahead and start reading her books right now:<br><br>•	Young Adult Novels<br>•	Science Fiction<br>•	Superheroes<br>•	Cheesy Love Stories (usually between an odd couple)<br><br>I feel like most of my Goodreads friends would find something to enjoy in this series, so if you are looking of a three book adventure with some action and some romance set in a super-hero/sci-fi world, you can safely put Supernova on your list!<br><br>Anyone have the Liz Phair song in your head now? No? Just me . . . okay . . .<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1583446279ra/29062363.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_3009326886" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3009326886" />
    <a title="Jasmine from How Useful It Is" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4467515-jasmine-from-how-useful-it-is"><img alt="Jasmine from How Useful It Is" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1516737798p2/4467515.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3009326886?book_show_action=true">Mar 18, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jasmine from How Useful It Is" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jasmine from How Useful It Is" href="/user/show/4467515-jasmine-from-how-useful-it-is">Jasmine from How Useful It Is</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4467515-jasmine-from-how-useful-it-is?shelf=library">library</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4467515-jasmine-from-how-useful-it-is?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4467515-jasmine-from-how-useful-it-is?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3009326886" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15420112601170896380">I'm reading this book while in the hospital getting treatment for pneumonia. The cough is keeping me up so I might as well enjoy the actions and adventures of Nova and her villains. I'm liking this book a lot more. I like how quick the villains think. They speak so little and let silence stretches on but they all come to the same conclusion that time is running out and they need to act fast. I like their teamwork, how different they are but they work well together. Honey's humor is always a plus</span>
  <span id="freeText15420112601170896380" style="display:none">I'm reading this book while in the hospital getting treatment for pneumonia. The cough is keeping me up so I might as well enjoy the actions and adventures of Nova and her villains. I'm liking this book a lot more. I like how quick the villains think. They speak so little and let silence stretches on but they all come to the same conclusion that time is running out and they need to act fast. I like their teamwork, how different they are but they work well together. Honey's humor is always a plus even if it brings scowls out of Nova. I love the butterflies - Danna and how she knows who the spy is but couldn't get her triumphant moment but still swarm over with her multiple numbers of butterflies. I like Adrian's puzzle solving of Nightmare and his conclusion. I like Oscar's grand guestures for professing his love no matter how hopeless it seems. He sure goes above and beyond. I enjoy Nova and the adrenaline rush surrounding her double life and fear of lies unraveling.<br /><br /> This book is told in the third person point of view following Nova. Nova has just completed her mission from book 2, but not everything goes according to plans and so she's back at headquarters doing her spy job as a Renegade. No sooner then she received a threatening message at her home blackmailing for her identity to turning in Ace's helmet. When Nova's secret of being a spy revealed, she found herself going to prison where her uncle and top villains Ace's has been. The alternating view is Adrian, who could draw anything into reality, is living a secret double life of his own. Adrian is the adopted son of the famous Renegades dads. His desperation to find Nightmare is ever increasing. At first he wanted to find her to learn about his mom's death but now he wanted to find her to kill her because he believed she meant to kill his half brother Max. The adventures moved on to rescuing Ace at his execution.<br /><br /> Supernova is very well written and a fast paced read. I loved the attack on the Renegades with the bees and the rescue of Ace. Pretty cool scene. I like Queen Bee's power over all of the stingers. They sure can do some damages. Phobia is scary, a definite character for the villains. I like his mystery. I love the battle with Ace the Anarchist. The love story is mostly innocent with few kisses the entire series so it's readable for any readers middle grade and young adults. Overall, I enjoyed the series and recommend everyone to read Renegade series.<br /><br />xoxo, Jasmine at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.howusefulitis.wordpress.com">www.howusefulitis.wordpress.com</a> for more details <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15420112601170896380" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="beth ✨" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/72715251-beth"><img alt="beth ✨" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1600471872p2/72715251.jpg" /></a>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer657468675843098312">We have a cover. I REPEAT, we have a cover. It is absolutely stunning and my favourite in the series. Nova is the QUEEN. 🤷🏻‍♀️😍<br/><br/><br/>////////////<br/><br/>hi hello <br/><br/>marissa meyer i will give anything to have an arc of this in my hands asap?? i will give my firstborn???</span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2592188422" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2592188422" />
    <a title="Safia  (safiabooknerd)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/67443309-safia-safiabooknerd"><img alt="Safia  (safiabooknerd)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1563049385p2/67443309.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2592188422?book_show_action=true">Nov 12, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Safia  (safiabooknerd)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Safia  (safiabooknerd)" href="/user/show/67443309-safia-safiabooknerd">Safia  (safiabooknerd)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2592188422" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3501437356622223825"><b>This book fell so flat for me</b>. <br/><br/>I was so excited for this book and I really expected more from it. This book had an insane amount of hype and wasn't the "epic conclusion" that it was trying so hard to be. <b>*Sigh*</b>. This is what I get for my hardcore fangirling. <br/><br/><b>The plot:</b><br/>What even was the plot? I was so confused in the first half of the book. Everything was so unbelievably dull and didn't pick up with the same action and intensity that we were left off at with <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/35425827.Archenemies__Renegades___2_' title='Archenemies (Renegades, #2) by Marissa Meyer' rel='nofollow noopener'>Archenemies</a>. I think we should all get </span>
  <span id="freeText3501437356622223825" style="display:none"><b>This book fell so flat for me</b>. <br><br>I was so excited for this book and I really expected more from it. This book had an insane amount of hype and wasn't the "epic conclusion" that it was trying so hard to be. <b>*Sigh*</b>. This is what I get for my hardcore fangirling. <br><br><b>The plot:</b><br>What even was the plot? I was so confused in the first half of the book. Everything was so unbelievably dull and didn't pick up with the same action and intensity that we were left off at with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/35425827.Archenemies__Renegades___2_" title="Archenemies (Renegades, #2) by Marissa Meyer" rel="nofollow noopener">Archenemies</a>. I think we should all get together in one collective <i>cringe</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1583086372ra/29043226.gif" width="”275″" height="”325″" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Dear lord, the amount of cringe in this book… Okay, all of the books in this trilogy were tinged with a bit of cringe, but I kind of expected that. The trilogy gets its inspiration from comic books and superpowers, I expected some lame humor. But the amount of lame one liners, cheesy romance parts and cliche oh-so-predictable scenes made me roll my eyes so hard that I can see the back of my freaking brain. This book went from having a resemblance to a comic book to actually sounding like a lame, PG, barely interesting, kids comic book. I guess the only reason I kept reading and didn’t give up because of the cringe was because I was curious to see how things would end for Adrian and Nova. <br><br>There was a major plot twist in this book which is what saved it from being a 2 star read for me. But it wasn’t enough to make me more than mildly like it. When I finished reading the book, I kept on thinking “What happened?” A lot of the action and fun parts were minimal and a lot of things felt unnecessary. There were a few backstories interwoven throughout the book, but they seemed more interesting than the actual book. Everything that was done in the book felt a bit redundant, and to be honest, it was better done in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28421168.Renegades__Renegades___1_" title="Renegades (Renegades, #1) by Marissa Meyer" rel="nofollow noopener">Renegades</a>. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1582996944ra/29038097.gif" height="”325″" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I hate when trilogies end with an annoying/unnecessary cliffhanger or piece of info. Like okay, I see that cash grab. There was a piece of info at the end that irritated me so much. Yes, it’s exciting. BUT I COULD HAVE LIVED WITHOUT IT. It’s clear that the little bit of a cliffhanger that was left was just enough to set the premise for another book. A final book is just supposed to be that - final. An ending. Not the premise/starting point for a new book or series. <br><br><b>The characters:</b><br>Even our amazing side characters like Oscar weren’t enough to save this book from the awful character development. I don’t even know what happened. Everyone just turned to mush in this book and I feel like the author was desperately trying to make sure she fulfilled everyone’s hopes in regards to who the characters will end up with romantically. <br><br><b>Nova:</b><br>Nova. Nova, Nova, Nova. Tsk, tsk, tsk. Nova was just plain irritating. It was so hard to understand what Nova wanted. Heck, it looked like she was confusing HERSELF with all of her indecisiveness. She didn’t know who she was doing her bad lying to and for, and the amount of gaslighting she did was so headache inducing. It wasn’t just the bad lying that annoyed me, it was the <i>nature</i> of her lies. Flimsy and so stupid. Does she think everyone was born yesterday? PEOPLE ARE NOT DUMB THEY CAN FIGURE SH*T OUT lol. Nova was never consistent and she let all of her lovey feelings for Adrian get in the way of everything. I just wanted to scream “PICK A FREAKING SIDE!” at her. Nova’s that person that would be torturous to eat out with because she’s the kind of person that takes an hour to order food, but then decides on a burger and fries. Boring. <br><br><b>Adrian:</b><br>I guess Adrian was alright, but he was so unbelievably offhand and dull without Nova. I just wanted to skip through his chapters because they were boring at times. He has an uncanny ability to irritate me with his good guy narrative and his recklessness around Max. <br><br><b>The romance:</b><br>The romance felt so stupid. There was so much sappy and cringey stuff happening. After everything, nothing about the romance seemed realistic (I don’t want to reveal too much because I might spoil it). <br><br>I guess this book had a <i>really</i> rocky start, but it ended okay. I like the trilogy, but with this book it feels like the author was scrambling to tie up some loose ends but ended up forgetting some things. I still feel confused, and I don’t know why, but I feel those weird unsettled and not content feelings like something’s missing. I can’t help but feel like the cliche ending that this book had could ever be possible in a place like Gatlon. There were a bunch of outlandish and strange parts too. It felt like I was watching people shuffle through a rehearsed and predictable play. <br><br>The last two books isn’t this trilogy ruined it for me. Everything was better done in Renegades. The trilogy has an interesting concept, but terrible execution.<br><br><b>Pre-review (you can skip it if you want):</b><br>I can't <i>breathe</i>, the cover is absolutely STUNNING.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1577469593i/28675841._SX540_.jpg" width="”275″" height="”325″" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>(No, that is not my image. I found it on the internet lol)</b><br><br>Honestly, forget everything I said before about me not living for the cover. I'm living and breathing for this cover (does that sound creepy? I don't know lol). How dare I doubt Marissa Meyer. She never disappoints. That cover is GORGEOUS and has exceeded all of my expectations. I can't wait until November!<br><br><b>4/28/19:</b><br><b>Supernova?</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1552963674ra/27227933.gif" height="”325″" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>SUPER FREAKING NOVA?! What the hell? I'm beyond disappointed in this title. It sounds <i>cheesy</i>. Also, why is Nova's name in the title? I'm not a fan of it. Since there's a book named after the Renegades I was expecting the last one to be named after the Anarchists. Just...what the fudge is going on? When I first saw the title, it was 2 A.M, I was pretty mad, and everything you're about to read is my initial reaction.<br><br><b>WARNING! HEAVY SPOILERS FOR <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28421168.Renegades__Renegades___1_" title="Renegades (Renegades, #1) by Marissa Meyer" rel="nofollow noopener">Renegades</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/35425827.Archenemies__Renegades___2_" title="Archenemies (Renegades, #2) by Marissa Meyer" rel="nofollow noopener">Archenemies</a>!</b><br><br><br>I needed to refresh myself on what <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/35425827.Archenemies__Renegades___2_" title="Archenemies (Renegades, #2) by Marissa Meyer" rel="nofollow noopener">Archenemies</a> was about and I read my review. Let me tell you, I'm crinnnnging at my review for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/35425827.Archenemies__Renegades___2_" title="Archenemies (Renegades, #2) by Marissa Meyer" rel="nofollow noopener">Archenemies</a>. It's. Just. So. Fangirly. I just remember hyperventilating after I read it. Now I know better, and I let my feelings about a book settle down and I let the fangirly smoke clear before I write a review.<br><br>Okay, okay, it's time for theories:<br><br> - <b>If Adrian doesn't find out about Nova's little secret, I will riot.</b><br> We can't end the trilogy without everyone being exposed and my book-loving heart breaking open. That's how it was for the first two books, anyway. I'm starting to suspect a pattern.<br><br> - <b>I think Phobia killed Lady Indomitable (Adrian's mom)?</b><br>He seems to really like the quote "One cannot be brave who has no fear". Ummm...Phobia...sweetie, I think you just exposed yourself. That quote was found on Lady Indomitable's corpse. I’m pretty sure that someone who can fly has a fear of falling. Maybe Lady Indomitable was lacking that fear and Phobia decided to intervene and do something about it...<br><br> - <b>Maybe Ace is working against Nova? Maybe he's using Nova?</b><br>He needs Nova to get that helmet. Maybe he sees her as a means to an end. Ace gives me bad vibes, and Nova is devoted to helping him. He seems distant from his only niece.<br><br> - <b>The Puppeteer will snitch</b><br>I mean... how much longer is he going to hold it in? Is he waiting for the right moment or what? Orrr he could <i>blackmail</i> Nova! That would be insaaane! He does his mind controll-y stuff to kids, so I don't think he's above blackmail lol. If he <i>does</i> decide to snitch, the Anarchists can't really make him pay because he used to be FaMiLy. The only person that could is the Detonator, but she's dead.<br><br> - <b>Adrian and Nova will probably break up</b> (were they even dating in the first place?) because Adrian will find out that Nova is Nightmare and Nova will find out that Adrian is the Sentinel. Oh my gosh! I'm freaking out just thinking about it! Buuut they probably won't report it to the Council because they still care for each other and they're silently going through a love/hate phase in their relationship.<br>I know. I ship them to no end.<br><br>Also, totally unrelated, but I just want things to be crystal clear. I totally stan Oscar. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1552963808ra/27227937.gif" width="”275″" height="”220" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Can we talk about the - dare I say- <i>subapar</i> (old) cover art?</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1565309663i/27958719._SY540_.jpg" width="”275″" height="”325″" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>*Gasp!* Shun me! I know! But I'm not living for the cover and it's seriously bothering me. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28421168.Renegades__Renegades___1_" title="Renegades (Renegades, #1) by Marissa Meyer" rel="nofollow noopener">Renegades</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/35425827.Archenemies__Renegades___2_" title="Archenemies (Renegades, #2) by Marissa Meyer" rel="nofollow noopener">Archenemies</a> had these really cool covers that look straight off of a comic book. This is just a blue background that's written in comic book font. Yikes. I hope that it'll be fixed when the book gets closer to its publication date.<br><br>All I know right now is that this book is going to be <b>messy</b> because of Nova's little secret. We'll either have a super long book (which I wouldn't mind) or we'll be blessed with another book.<br><br>I have high expectations. Stay tuned...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1552963960ra/27227948.gif" width="”275″" height="”325″" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>11/12/18:</b><br>Are three books really enough to capture all of the amazingness (Yes, I know that isn’t a word and I quite frankly don’t care) that is this trilogy ? I wouldn’t mind if this becomes a series. I <i>need</i> more of the Renegades world.</span>

<div id="review_2859561396" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2859561396" />
    <a title="Denzel." class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/75166110-denzel"><img alt="Denzel." src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577855459p2/75166110.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2859561396?book_show_action=true">Jan 26, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Denzel." class="user" itemprop="url" name="Denzel." href="/user/show/75166110-denzel">Denzel.</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/75166110-denzel?shelf=2020-reads">2020-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/75166110-denzel?shelf=4-stars">4-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2859561396" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17059066364669639986">”one can not be afraid when they have nothing to lose.” <br/><br/>"Everyone has a nightmare...Maybe I want you to be mine." <br/><br/>Imagine the renegades books adapted into films?? Yes. A blockbuster, action packed superhero film would be an awesome film. Definitely would watch. <br/><br/>Renegades synopsis: Galton city is invested with both good and evil. We have our renegades who are a council of superheroes fighting evil in their city, protecting the city. Then we have our anarchists, the villians that cause conflict an</span>
  <span id="freeText17059066364669639986" style="display:none">”one can not be afraid when they have nothing to lose.” <br /><br />"Everyone has a nightmare...Maybe I want you to be mine." <br /><br />Imagine the renegades books adapted into films?? Yes. A blockbuster, action packed superhero film would be an awesome film. Definitely would watch. <br /><br />Renegades synopsis: Galton city is invested with both good and evil. We have our renegades who are a council of superheroes fighting evil in their city, protecting the city. Then we have our anarchists, the villians that cause conflict and harm to the city. Nova artino is an anarchist and dispises the renegades, since they weren't there to protect her family when they died. She joins the renegades as undercover spy, to take them down from the inside.<br /><br />I thoroughly enjoyed the conclusion to the renegades trilogy. It ended smoothly and satisfyingly. The plot went in a direction I didn't expect which was amusing to read about. The twists and turns were unexpecting and I loved the thrill of it. I enjoyed the action and build-up towards the ending of the book, the battle/fight scene was delightful and captivating. I was never a huge fan of Nova and Adrian's relationship, I like them both very much as individuals more than them together, but in this book, I've really grown attached to their relationship. <br /><br />Wish we got more content from the side characters; Ruby, Donna, Oscar, Magpie and Max. Because after the ending of the book I really wanted to know about what they were up to or how they were doing. Magpie has been small but a valid character since book 1 and she was only mentioned once and that was when she was injured during a fight and then you never read about her or got any information regarding her character. Wanted to see some sort of relationship between Nova and Donna since of their estranged friendship, never got a clear understanding of them two as friends, only that Donna doesn't trust her because of what happened in book 2. Oscar and Ruby established a relationship, but it was just thrown into the storyline and wasn't necessary and didn't add anything to the plot. <br />All-around sad to say goodbye to these characters and story, but hoping we get some more content after that epilogue?!?! <br />I need to pick up her lunar chronicles series soon!</span>

<div id="review_2659577113" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2659577113" />
    <a title="Krystal" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18989854-krystal"><img alt="Krystal" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1491478087p2/18989854.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2659577113?book_show_action=true">Jan 11, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Krystal" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Krystal" href="/user/show/18989854-krystal">Krystal</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18989854-krystal?shelf=light-fantasy">light-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18989854-krystal?shelf=action-adventure">action-adventure</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18989854-krystal?shelf=motley-crew">motley-crew</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18989854-krystal?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18989854-krystal?shelf=owned">owned</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18989854-krystal?shelf=myths-legends-and-retellings">myths-legends-and-retellings</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2659577113" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10261134547562208392"><b>THIS HAS BEEN THE MOST INTENSE DAY OF READING I'VE HAD ALL YEAR.</b><br/><br/>WHAT A RUSH.<br/><br/><i>Where do I even start?</i><br/><br/>Obviously I loved it. The first two books set things up so well, so there were plenty of questions and theories waiting for answers and confrontations waiting to happen. <br/><br/><u>WARNING: This review contains spoilers for the first two books in the series.</u><br/><br/>Firstly, I was really glad this book contained gentle reminders of what happened in the last book(s) because it meant I didn't have to waste time trying to</span>
  <span id="freeText10261134547562208392" style="display:none"><b>THIS HAS BEEN THE MOST INTENSE DAY OF READING I'VE HAD ALL YEAR.</b><br /><br />WHAT A RUSH.<br /><br /><i>Where do I even start?</i><br /><br />Obviously I loved it. The first two books set things up so well, so there were plenty of questions and theories waiting for answers and confrontations waiting to happen. <br /><br /><u>WARNING: This review contains spoilers for the first two books in the series.</u><br /><br />Firstly, I was really glad this book contained gentle reminders of what happened in the last book(s) because it meant I didn't have to waste time trying to remember the important things. Sometimes you waste a couple chapters trying to get back into the flow of a story you haven't read in a year or so and it can be frustrating, whereas this throws you back in with all the important tidbits to make sure you're up to speed.<br /><br />Then <b>the action comes and it doesn't stop coming.</b><br /><br />Nova is so badass, and she's determined to do what she thinks is right, no matter how many moral lines she has to cross. Poor, duped Adrian. She loves the guy, but she's still messing with that pretty head of his. Bless his determination to believe the best of everyone.<br /><br />I really don't like Danna, and I wish there was more animosity between her and Nova but they're so damn forgiving. Blegh. But at least there is the nastiness between Nova and Magpie and that really makes my heart soar. It's a dynamic that was unexpected but I've grown to love it over these three books. Ruby and Oscar are adorable and funny and help lighten the mood when things are getting too serious. Ruby's brothers are a manic energy I can really get behind. Max is chill, and his childlike mind creates a strange balance to this world of violence.<br /><br />When the Nightmare reveal came it was not nearly as dramatic as I was expecting, considering it's been building for two books. Everyone handled it much better than I thought they would. The council were douchebags, of course, but that's to be expected. Massive egos on that bunch of weirdos.<br /><br />There were also some really interesting answers to burning questions and I am happy to finally have closure. It was a fun journey to kinda experience the unfolding of all the secrets and lies, particularly since it was peppered through all the action. There were no annoying walls of explanations or long-winded speeches. Everything was revealed so naturally.<br /><br />This book is also an adventure in its own right. There are more barriers to overcome and Nova and Adrian both have a few things they need to work out about how they see the world. That's something I've really enjoyed over the course of this series - the heroes vs the villains and all of the grey in between. Right and wrong and who decides what that is. What makes people special, what makes a hero. Big questions with no clear answers.<br /><br />The drama got pretty intense and there was a lot that I was definitely not expecting that tugged my heart a bit! It was such a fun romp that I wasn't expecting to <i>feel</i> so much. <b>Why you make me get all attached, Marissa Meyer? </b><br /><br />But fear not - there is still a ton of action with explosions, fight scenes, chases, etc so you will definitely not get bored or waste too much time sitting around contemplating your <i>feelings</i>. <br /><br />A worthy conclusion to the series, but one that definitely leaves it open for a spin-off, which I 1000% support. Bring me those dastardly villains and their plots any time.<br /><br />***<br /><br />Review for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28421168.Renegades__Renegades___1_" title="Renegades (Renegades, #1) by Marissa Meyer" rel="nofollow noopener">Renegades</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2178859627" rel="nofollow noopener">HERE</a><br />Review for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/35425827.Archenemies__Renegades___2_" title="Archenemies (Renegades, #2) by Marissa Meyer" rel="nofollow noopener">Archenemies</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2622853747" rel="nofollow noopener">HERE</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="10261134547562208392" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2620783233" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17260483316709708002"><b>4.5 stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462551983ra/19013225.gif' width='400' height='300' alt='' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>WOW.<br/><br/>Seriously...WOW<br/><br/>I feel speechless by how much this book has me shook right now. I am in no way exaggerating when I say this book had me on a rollercoaster ride of emotions. There were times where I genuinely thought I would rate this 2 stars because I was so furious with the plot and where things were going, and then every time I thought I knew what was going to happen, Marissa Meyer threw another plot twist and left me shocked and scrambling to figure out how I felt. Happy, sad, ang</span>
  <span id="freeText17260483316709708002" style="display:none"><b>4.5 stars</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462551983ra/19013225.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>WOW.<br><br>Seriously...WOW<br><br>I feel speechless by how much this book has me shook right now. I am in no way exaggerating when I say this book had me on a rollercoaster ride of emotions. There were times where I genuinely thought I would rate this 2 stars because I was so furious with the plot and where things were going, and then every time I thought I knew what was going to happen, Marissa Meyer threw another plot twist and left me shocked and scrambling to figure out how I felt. Happy, sad, angry, excited, frustrated, distraught...I felt every single one of these feelings and many more countless times while reading this 500 page book. There were times where I felt like I wanted to put it down because I just didn't know how much more I could handle, I was scared for these characters and I was worried they wouldn't get a satisfying ending. And while this book definitely didn't make things easy...the ending was well worth the anxiety-induced ball of stress I became while I read this. <br><br>That ending, the plot twist, the way everything connected together...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383774976ra/6663557.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This author is a freaking genius and I feel both dumb for never making the connections and also eager to pick her mind and see what else she has in store for these characters and this world. <br><br>I do have small complaints, mainly that I feel like this was a much more plot heavy book (which makes sense given that it's the last book and there was lots that needed to happen) but I missed the character and romance drivenness of the first two books (especially the second). I wish we'd gotten more of Adrian and Nova's relationship, especially at the end. I wanted more and I'm hoping we'll be getting a novella bind up again like we did with the Lunar Chronicles because I am in no way ready to say goodbye to them or any of these characters. <br><br>This book is a winner and Marissa truly showed us that she knows how to write a great conclusion to a series!</span>
  <a data-text-id="17260483316709708002" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2592598439" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2592598439" />
    <a title="Prerana" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/33062312-prerana"><img alt="Prerana" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603914295p2/33062312.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2592598439?book_show_action=true">Nov 06, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Prerana" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Prerana" href="/user/show/33062312-prerana">Prerana</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33062312-prerana?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33062312-prerana?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2592598439" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9213368484368134938">What. Complete. And. Utter. Trash.<br/><br/>I am genuinely disappointed after how much I had enjoyed the first two books. This novel was such a colossal letdown that I honestly am at a mild loss for words.<br/><br/>This book was an absolute fucking trainwreck. I was eager for a conclusion that would clinch together the internal and external struggle that had been brewing since the first book. I wanted to see the dilemma of good vs. evil, of how lines aren't as black and white as they initially seem, how things don'</span>
  <span id="freeText9213368484368134938" style="display:none">What. Complete. And. Utter. Trash.<br /><br />I am genuinely disappointed after how much I had enjoyed the first two books. This novel was such a colossal letdown that I honestly am at a mild loss for words.<br /><br />This book was an absolute fucking trainwreck. I was eager for a conclusion that would clinch together the internal and external struggle that had been brewing since the first book. I wanted to see the dilemma of good vs. evil, of how lines aren't as black and white as they initially seem, how things don't always end well. <br /><br />Yeah, absolutely none of that happened. <br /><br />This was a slew of one mistake after another. The first two books had soared on the strengths of the characters. Supernova completely destroyed any character development that any of them had going on. I don't even know what to say because it was so bad. Both Nova and Adrian had such random changes of heart. They were put in situations that literally don't even make any sense and then made choices that were completely out of character for how they had been characterized throughout the entire series. <br /><br />I also felt distinctly preached at. I absolutely hate that. If you don't know how much I hate it, go ahead and read my review of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11337.The_Bluest_Eye" title="The Bluest Eye by Toni Morrison" rel="nofollow noopener">The Bluest Eye</a>. I hate it.<br /><br />I don't want to be told about whatever moral or lesson you're trying to teach me. How does that convince me to follow your advice? No, I want you to <i>show</i> me. Give me examples, show me the consequences of not following your advice, make me empathize with people who might face similar choices. <br /><br />Convince me why your lesson is important.<br /><br />And I genuinely thought Marissa Meyer might actually do that with this series. The first two books were shaping up so brilliantly with this beautiful struggle of what truly is heroism and what is the actual difference between good and evil. Who are the villains?<br /><br />And this book completely fucked everything over. <br /><br />There were literally passages, chapters even, where Meyer just crusaded about this. And literally none of the characters demonstrated anything she was trying to put out. Nova was distinctly unlikeable in this; she made some very unsavory choices that were not born of any particular struggle or reason. But somehow everything becomes magically resolved?<br /><br />None of the plot twists were particularly surprising, yet they were all jarring because very few contributed to the depth of the plot. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Like, wow, who didn't see it coming that Ace did not have anyone's best interests at heart? And oh, some of the good guys are villains, and some of the bad guys are heroes. Wow. So original. Oh, and wow, Narcissa pretends to be Nightmare.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />But then some other shit happens, and the characters just conveniently ignore it? <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Nova literally tries to kill Adrian. She lets Honey torture him (yeah, the book didn't label it as torture but tell me that cutting your skin off with a knife is not torture), and then Adrian is just like, oof I love you sweetie, it's okay you made all those bad decisions. And then Oscar and Danna are literally like, Nova has not done anything to make us trust her, she has lied this entire time. But Adrian's like, well I trust her, so you should too. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />I don't know, honestly. Marissa Meyer has consistently always let me down with her books, so maybe I was misguided in actually having expectations for this one. I have definitely learned my lesson (not the one she was trying to preach, though). I can't even believe it. I actually put the first two books of this series on my worth-re-reading shelf. What am I supposed to do now? Read the first two books of the series and then never finish it when I do a reread? Ugh. I hate series with bad conclusions. Regardless, I just don't think Marissa Meyer is for me.<br /><br />And I'm out.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9213368484368134938" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_3441635735" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3441635735" />
    <a title="Maria V. Snyder" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1629797-maria-v-snyder"><img alt="Maria V. Snyder" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1530814046p2/1629797.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3441635735?book_show_action=true">Jul 25, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maria V. Snyder" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maria V. Snyder" href="/user/show/1629797-maria-v-snyder">Maria V. Snyder</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3441635735" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13186984119984518819">I think this is my first two star review. I usually only review books that I love as authors have enough bad reviews to deal with and I don't want to add more. And this isn't a bad review...not really. It's a wish that the series had a stronger, more engaging, satisfying ending. And it also may be due to the fact that I'm a writer and a teacher of writing - I saw SO MUCH potential here - and the possibility of huge emotional scenes that were set up perfectly and just didn't occur. Perhaps Meyer </span>
  <span id="freeText13186984119984518819" style="display:none">I think this is my first two star review. I usually only review books that I love as authors have enough bad reviews to deal with and I don't want to add more. And this isn't a bad review...not really. It's a wish that the series had a stronger, more engaging, satisfying ending. And it also may be due to the fact that I'm a writer and a teacher of writing - I saw SO MUCH potential here - and the possibility of huge emotional scenes that were set up perfectly and just didn't occur. Perhaps Meyer ran out of pages - although a good editor could have helped with that (see my comments in the spoiler).<br /><br />The series is wonderful because of the characters and world. Meyer does a great job of making the readers love both main protagonists and hope they both win, which, considering they are archenemies is a hard thing to pull it off. So kudos to her for doing that! Five stars for the characters! Five stars for the richly detailed world.<br /><br />The rest I'm going to hide as a spoiler. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[A few things that failed for me: One - Nova as Nightmare - the clues were all there. She did a ton of stupid things to tip them off. It was obvious, yet two Council members and Adrian failed to put them together. And when it finally was revealed...there's a weak attempt to make it appear Narcissa is Nightmare. Come on! Adrian and his Dads are supposedly intelligent people! Adrian might be in denial, but, come on! He fell asleep while kissing her!! I lost a ton of respect for the Renegades at that point. And then she's released from prison? What was the point of putting her in there? What is the author trying to show? That the place is horrible and these people shouldn't be there - okay, but that could be done in a couple paragraphs. Why go to all the trouble of having her arrested only to release her and do the entire, "She's a spy" thing again. Better to skip all that - and spend the pages on other, more engaging emotional scenes that weren't there.<br /><br />What scenes? I'm glad you asked ;) Adrian as the Sentinel - he spends two books hiding who he is and then when it's revealed it's a non issue. Even Nova is like, "whatever." There's no conversation with his Dads, no realization that the Council might be getting a bit too dictatorial. Wouldn't it been cool if Nova and Adrian revealed their alter egos at the same time to each other? I know it was done so well in Buffy the Vampire Slayer, but with the set up of these books, it could have been done in Meyer's own way. Another missing scene Adrian dealing with the fact he created Phobia!! Yes, he struggles with it a bit and then sacrifices his superpowers, but that's HUGE! The readers needed to see him grappling with that one since Phobia killed his mother - in fact Adrian killed her because of his fears - yes, he was just a young boy, but still! And the reveal about Ace killing Nova's family. Would like to see her dealing with that a little longer and coming to the realization that she'd been blaming the Renegades all these years. Another scene: Ruby and Oscar - I realize they are minor characters, but still the readers have read about Oscar mooning over Ruby and then at the end they're holding hands - needed more there. And then there needs to be more about how the world will deal with everyone having superpowers. I admit - I didn't see that coming - I thought it would go the other way - no one had powers. There's mention that things will be different, but nothing else. Three books worth of how society is unbalanced and the people are too passive because they believe the Renegades will save them. I'd would have loved to see at least of hint of how society is now dealing with this. <br /> <br />And lastly - that epilogue! I didn't see that one either - that Magpie is Evie, Nova's baby sister that supposedly died. Does this mean there will be book 4? Why reveal that when nothing is going to happen. That could have come sooner - would have been nice to see Nova and Evie reunited. And it makes it appear that after all that fighting, deaths, Agent N, etc... nothing really has changed.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Like I said there was SO MUCH POTENTIAL to make this book a knock-your-socks-off whooper of a conclusion because the set up was all there and masterly done. The fact that I just typed up 3 paragraphs in the spoiler alone shows just how engaged I was in the story and characters! <br /><br />Thoughts? </span>
  <a data-text-id="13186984119984518819" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

		<td>
		    <b>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('xh09KdH9FNX1rdmtEQBJTB6CtGEvAWyxR67qY4zhv8Ar4wfEPQUlVyLd4wes/5V6yoscwpDplAmvzlR57/frEg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('LMpIhqSFqasSzBGVv3LCTIcp3Qsnn9ULg2b/MRT4/ebBNHJrSH2YKcW8Kz8CjR56UyB1qJh3LbNrBkErd+6pNA==')})
  }
